</li>
<li id="cite_note-92"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-92">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">There are no invariants under the <a href="/wiki/General_linear_group" title="General linear group">general linear group</a> of all invertible linear transformations because these transformations can be multiplication by a scaling factor. To remedy this, classical invariant theory also considered <i>relative invariants</i>, which were forms invariant up to a scale factor.</span>
</li>

<h3><span id="Selected_works_by_Emmy_Noether_.28in_German.29"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Selected_works_by_Emmy_Noether_(in_German)">Selected works by Emmy Noether (in German)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Emmy_Noether&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Selected works by Emmy Noether (in German)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1033289096" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/List_of_publications_by_Emmy_Noether" title="List of publications by Emmy Noether">List of publications by Emmy Noether</a></div>
<ul><li><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1067248974" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><cite class="citation cs2 cs1-prop-foreign-lang-source" id="CITEREFNoether1908">Noether, Emmy (1908), <a class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20130308102907/http://gdz.sub.uni-goettingen.de/no_cache/dms/load/img/?IDDOC=261200" rel="nofollow">"Über die Bildung des Formensystems der ternären biquadratischen Form"</a> [On Complete Systems of Invariants for Ternary Biquadratic Forms], <i>Journal für die Reine und Angewandte Mathematik</i> (in German), <a href="/wiki/Germany" title="Germany">DE</a>, <b>1908</b> (134): 23–90 and two tables, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Doi_(identifier)" title="Doi (identifier)">doi</a>:<a class="external text" href="https://doi.org/10.1515%2Fcrll.1908.134.23" rel="nofollow">10.1515/crll.1908.134.23</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/S2CID_(identifier)" title="S2CID (identifier)">S2CID</a> <a class="external text" href="https://api.semanticscholar.org/CorpusID:119967160" rel="nofollow">119967160</a>, archived from <a class="external text" href="http://gdz.sub.uni-goettingen.de/no_cache/dms/load/img/?IDDOC=261200" rel="nofollow">the original</a> on 8 March 2013</cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Ajournal&amp;rft.genre=article&amp;rft.jtitle=Journal+f%C3%BCr+die+Reine+und+Angewandte+Mathematik&amp;rft.atitle=%C3%9Cber+die+Bildung+des+Formensystems+der+tern%C3%A4ren+biquadratischen+Form&amp;rft.volume=1908&amp;rft.issue=134&amp;rft.pages=23-90+and+two+tables&amp;rft.date=1908&amp;rft_id=info%3Adoi%2F10.1515%2Fcrll.1908.134.23&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Fapi.semanticscholar.org%2FCorpusID%3A119967160%23id-name%3DS2CID&amp;rft.aulast=Noether&amp;rft.aufirst=Emmy&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fgdz.sub.uni-goettingen.de%2Fno_cache%2Fdms%2Fload%2Fimg%2F%3FIDDOC%3D261200&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AEmmy+Noether"></span></li>
<li><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1067248974" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><cite class="citation cs2 cs1-prop-foreign-lang-source" id="CITEREFNoether1913">——— (1913), <a class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20130308102912/http://gdz.sub.uni-goettingen.de/no_cache/dms/load/img/?IDDOC=244058" rel="nofollow">"Rationale Funktionenkörper"</a> [Rational Function Fields], <i>J. <ul><li><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1067248974" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><cite class="citation cs2 cs1-prop-foreign-lang-source"><a class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20070929100418/http://www.physikerinnen.de/noetherlebenslauf.html" rel="nofollow"><i>Noether Lebensläufe</i></a> (in German), <a href="/wiki/Germany" title="Germany">DE</a>: Physikerinnen, archived from <a class="external text" href="http://www.physikerinnen.de/noetherlebenslauf.html" rel="nofollow">the original</a> on 29 September 2007<span class="reference-accessdate">, retrieved <span class="nowrap">20 October</span> 2006</span></cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.btitle=Noether+Lebensl%C3%A4ufe&amp;rft.place=DE&amp;rft.pub=Physikerinnen&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.physikerinnen.de%2Fnoetherlebenslauf.html&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AEmmy+Noether"></span>. Noether's application for admission to the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/University_of_Erlangen" title="University of Erlangen">University of Erlangen</a> and three <a href="/wiki/Curriculum_vitae" title="Curriculum vitae">curricula vitae</a>, two of which are shown in handwriting, with transcriptions. The first of these is in Emmy Noether's own handwriting.</li>
<li><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1067248974" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><cite class="citation web cs1"><a class="external text" href="http://triarte.brynmawr.edu/Obj188672?sid=318669&amp;x=31763306" rel="nofollow">"Letter from Emmy Noether to Dr. Marion Edwards Park, President of Bryn Mawr College"</a>. <i>TriArte</i>.
